password1
## paste public key to authorized keys for user asamadhi

ssh Please type 'yes', 'no' or the fingerprint: asamadhi@100.71.227.145  "chmod 600 /Users/asamadhi/.ssh/authorized_keys"

ssh asamadhi@100.71.227.145  "ls -la  /Users/asamadhi/.ssh/"
password1

## Add config entry for jumphost
cat ~/.ssh/config
cat << 'EOF' >>  ~/.ssh/config
Host jumphost
     IdentitiesOnly yes
     IdentityFile ~/.ssh/lab_key
     Hostname 100.71.227.145
     User asamadhi
EOF

# Test ssh trust
ssh -i ~/.ssh/lab_key asamadhi@100.71.227.145  "whoami; hostname; date"
ssh jumphost  "whoami; hostname; date"

### Access via JumpHost

## Add config entry for centos VM
cat ~/.ssh/config
cat << 'EOF' >>  ~/.ssh/config
Host centos_parallels
     IdentitiesOnly yes
     IdentityFile ~/.ssh/lab_key
     Hostname 10.211.55.3
     User parallels
     ProxyJump jumphost
Host centos_wls
     IdentitiesOnly yes
     IdentityFile ~/.ssh/lab_key
     Hostname 10.211.55.3
     User wls
     ProxyJump jumphost
EOF

## Test direct access to centos VM via jumphost Please type 'yes', 'no' or the fingerprint: using config file
ssh centos_parallels "whoami; hostname; pwd"
ssh centos_wls "whoami; hostname; pwd"
